## זְאֵב (id: 001910000000000)

זְאֵב
=====

זְאֵב (H2061 · H2062)

noun m

Wild Animals

wolf \= wild, four\-footed, predatory canine; light\-brown fur, similar to jackal, but much bigger; ◄ Canis lupus; ► commonly prey on flocks; ≈ regarded as ravenous and fierce; symbol of roaming, opportunistic, dangerous, fierce, and clever banditry

[GEN 49:27](https://ref.ly/Gen49:27) · [ISA 11:6](https://ref.ly/Isa11:6) · [ISA 65:25](https://ref.ly/Isa65:25) · [JER 5:6](https://ref.ly/Jer5:6) · [EZK 22:27](https://ref.ly/Ezek22:27) · [HAB 1:8](https://ref.ly/Hab1:8) · [ZEP 3:3](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:3)

name

Names of People

Zeeb \= man; ► a chief of the Midianites, defeated and killed by Gideon

[JDG 7:25](https://ref.ly/Judg7:25) · [JDG 7:25](https://ref.ly/Judg7:25) · [JDG 7:25](https://ref.ly/Judg7:25) · [JDG 7:25](https://ref.ly/Judg7:25) · [JDG 8:3](https://ref.ly/Judg8:3) · [PSA 83:12](https://ref.ly/Ps83:12)

Lénart J. de Regt

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 49:27; Isaiah 11:6; Isaiah 65:25; Jeremiah 5:6; Ezekiel 22:27; Habakkuk 1:8; Zephaniah 3:3; Judges 7:25; Judges 8:3; Psalms 83:12


## זבד (id: 001911000000000)

זבד
===

זבד (H2064)

verb · אֶלְזָבָד · זָבָד · זַבְדִּי · זַבְדִּיאֵל · זְבַדְיָה · זְבַדְיָהוּ · זָבוּד · זבידה

Non\-Possess 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

**Collocation:** זבד זֵבֶד

to give a precious gift \= causative action by which a deity bestows a precious gift upon someone else

[GEN 30:20](https://ref.ly/Gen30:20)

Lénart J. de Regt; Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 30:20

## זָבָד (id: 001913000000000)

זָבָד
=====

זָבָד (H2066)

name · זבד

Names of People

Zabad \= man; ◄ descendant of Jerahmeel; tribe of Judah

[1CH 2:36](https://ref.ly/1Chr2:36) · [1CH 2:37](https://ref.ly/1Chr2:37)

Names of People

Zabad \= man; ◄ son of Tahath; tribe of Ephraim

[1CH 7:21](https://ref.ly/1Chr7:21)

Names of People

Zabad \= man; ◄ son of Ahlai; ► a warrior during the time of king David

[1CH 11:41](https://ref.ly/1Chr11:41)

Names of People 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ יֹוזָבָד

Zabad, Jozabad \= man, also known as Jozabad; ► son of Shimeath, an Ammonite woman; ► he was a servant of Joash, king of Judah, who murdered his master with the help of Jehozabad, son of Shimrith; both were later killed by Joash' successor Amaziah

[2CH 24:26](https://ref.ly/2Chr24:26)

Names of People

Zabad \= various men; ► married foreign wives; after exile

[EZR 10:27](https://ref.ly/Ezra10:27) · [EZR 10:33](https://ref.ly/Ezra10:33) · [EZR 10:43](https://ref.ly/Ezra10:43)

Lénart J. de Regt

* **Associated Passages:** 1 Chronicles 2:36; 1 Chronicles 2:37; 1 Chronicles 7:21; 1 Chronicles 11:41; 2 Chronicles 24:26; Ezra 10:27; Ezra 10:33; Ezra 10:43

## זְבוּב (id: 001918000000000)

זְבוּב
======

זְבוּב (H2070)

noun m

Swarming Creatures

fly \= an insect with large composite eyes and a single pair of wings; ◄ \|iMusca domestica\|i\*; ► these insects converge in swarms on (rotting) food, dung, and household garbage; ≈ associated with large quantities

[ECC 10:1](https://ref.ly/Eccl10:1) · [ISA 7:18](https://ref.ly/Isa7:18)

Lénart J. de Regt; Enio R. Mueller

* **Associated Passages:** Ecclesiastes 10:1; Isaiah 7:18

## זבח (id: 001923000000000)

זבח
===

זבח (H2076)

verb · זֶבַח

Dead 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

to slaughter, to kill \= causative action by which humans kill one or more animals, usually for food

[DEU 12:15](https://ref.ly/Deut12:15) · [DEU 12:21](https://ref.ly/Deut12:21) · [1SA 28:24](https://ref.ly/1Sam28:24) · [1KI 13:2](https://ref.ly/1Kgs13:2) · [1KI 19:21](https://ref.ly/1Kgs19:21) · [2KI 23:20](https://ref.ly/2Kgs23:20) · [2CH 18:2](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:2) · [EZK 34:3](https://ref.ly/Ezek34:3)

Sacrifice 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb pi 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ עלה · קטר · שׁחט

to sacrifice \= the human activity of killing one or more animals as a religious sacrifice; usually part of the animal is offered to the deity and part is eaten by the worshipers; often accompanied by the burning of incense

## זֶבַח (id: 001924000000000)

זֶבַח
=====

זֶבַח (H2077 · H2078)

noun m · זבח

Sacrifice 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ אִשֵּׁה · בְּכֹר · מִנְחָה · מַעֲשֵׂר · נֵדֶר · נֶסֶךְ · עֹלָה · שֶׁלֶם · תְּרוּמָה

sacrifice \= the human activity of killing one or more animals as a religious sacrifice; usually part of the animal is offered to the deity and the other part is eaten by the worshipers; often accompanied by the burning of incense

## זָהָב (id: 001936000000000)

זָהָב
=====

זָהָב (H2091)

noun m

Metals 

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ בְּדִיל · בַּרְזֶל · זָהָב · כֶּסֶף · כֶּתֶם · נְחֹשֶׁת · עֹופֶרֶת · פּוּךְ · פַּז · צִפּוּי

gold \= metal of a bright yellow color, ◄ found in rocks and alluvial deposits ► and used as a monetary standard and in jewellery and plating; ≈ associated with wealth, beauty, and prosperity

## זַיִת (id: 001972000000000)

זַיִת
=====

זַיִת (H2132)

noun m

Trees

olive tree \= tree reaching up to 10 m. high, but usually pruned to around 5 m.; its leaves are grayish green above, and whitish underneath; its fruit is about 2 cm. long and a bit more than 1 cm. thick with a hard stone inside and a soft skin that covers the oily flesh; ► its fruit is used for food and oil for cooking, for lamps, for rubbing on the body, for medicine, and for anointing; ≈ regarded as beautiful and associated with well\-being

## זֵכֶר (id: 001983000000000)

זֵכֶר
=====

זֵכֶר (H2143)

noun m · זכר

Know

remembrance, memory, renown \= process in which information that is stored in one's mind regarding someone or something is being reprocessed continually and/or repeatedly

[EXO 17:14](https://ref.ly/Exod17:14) · [DEU 25:19](https://ref.ly/Deut25:19) · [DEU 32:26](https://ref.ly/Deut32:26) · [EST 9:28](https://ref.ly/Esth9:28) · [PSA 9:7](https://ref.ly/Ps9:7) · [PSA 34:17](https://ref.ly/Ps34:17) · [PSA 109:15](https://ref.ly/Ps109:15) · [PSA 111:4](https://ref.ly/Ps111:4) · [PSA 112:6](https://ref.ly/Ps112:6) · [ECC 9:5](https://ref.ly/Eccl9:5) · [ISA 26:14](https://ref.ly/Isa26:14) · [HOS 14:8](https://ref.ly/Hos14:8)

|  |
| --- |

 ≈ שֵׁם

| --- |

 ≈ ידה · רנן

## זִכָּרֹון (id: 001986000000000)

זִכָּרֹון
=========

זִכָּרֹון (H2146)

noun m · זכר

Know

remembrance \= process by which humans retain knowledge of people from the past, or of things that have happened in the past

[NEH 2:20](https://ref.ly/Neh2:20) · [ECC 1:11](https://ref.ly/Eccl1:11) · [ECC 1:11](https://ref.ly/Eccl1:11) · [ECC 2:16](https://ref.ly/Eccl2:16)

Objects

reminder \= an object that serves as a reminder to humans or deities of things that have happened or need to be done

[EXO 13:9](https://ref.ly/Exod13:9) · [EXO 28:12](https://ref.ly/Exod28:12) · [EXO 28:12](https://ref.ly/Exod28:12) · [EXO 28:29](https://ref.ly/Exod28:29) · [EXO 30:16](https://ref.ly/Exod30:16) · [EXO 39:7](https://ref.ly/Exod39:7) · [NUM 5:15](https://ref.ly/Num5:15) · [NUM 5:18](https://ref.ly/Num5:18) · [NUM 10:10](https://ref.ly/Num10:10) · [NUM 17:5](https://ref.ly/Num17:5) · [NUM 31:54](https://ref.ly/Num31:54) · [JOS 4:7](https://ref.ly/Josh4:7) · [ISA 57:8](https://ref.ly/Isa57:8) · [ZEC 6:14](https://ref.ly/Zech6:14)

Time

remembrance \= a time for remembering

[EXO 12:14](https://ref.ly/Exod12:14) · [LEV 23:24](https://ref.ly/Lev23:24)

Scrolls

remembrance \= a document with information that is to be remembered

[EXO 17:14](https://ref.ly/Exod17:14) · [EST 6:1](https://ref.ly/Esth6:1) · [MAL 3:16](https://ref.ly/Mal3:16)

Wise

wise saying \= knowledge and experiences from the past, that normally qualify as accumulated wisdom

[JOB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Job13:12)

Reinier de Blois

[NUM 13:23](https://ref.ly/Num13:23) · [ISA 17:10](https://ref.ly/Isa17:10) · [EZK 15:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek15:2) · [NAM 2:3](https://ref.ly/Nah2:3)1

Revile 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal

**Collocation:** שׁלח אֶת־הַזְּמֹורָה אֶל־אַף

to hold the vine branch to the nose \> to insult literally: "to hold the vine branch to their nose (or: my nose)"; hence, possibly: \= to make an insulting gesture

[EZK 8:17](https://ref.ly/Ezek8:17)2

1 NAM 2:3 RSV NJPS NRSV ESV "branches" NIV "vines" \| REB "strength" 2 EZK 8:17 This could be a tiqqun sopherim by which אַפּי "my nose" was written as אַפָּם "their nose"

Reinier de Blois

People

| --- |

 ≈ רֹאשׁ

## זרע (id: 002061000000000)

זרע
===

verb · זֵרוּעַ · זֶרַע · זֵרְעֹנִים · מִזְרָע · זְרַע

Plant 

|  |
| --- |

 verb qal, verb nif, verb pu'al

to sow, to scatter, to plant \= action by which humans scatter seeds or plant young plants in a field so that they may grow into a new crop; ≈ associated with the concept of investing in order to get a return; also associated with reproduction and perpetuation
